add_namespace = ottoman

country_event = { #ottoman revolt
	id = ottoman.0
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		random_controlled_state = {
			limit = { resistance > 79.9 }
			controller = { set_temp_variable = { global.occupier_country = THIS } }
			set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_state = THIS }
			if = {
				limit = { has_resistance = yes }
				set_resistance = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = ALB }
			}
			ALB = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
				country_exists = ALB
				ALB = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = ALB
				copy_tag = ALB
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_albanian_minority }
					is_core_of = ALB
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ALB
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = ALB
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_core_of = IKR
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = IKR }
			}
			IKR = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = GRE_greek_resistance
					days = 365
				}
				add_ideas = standing_alone
				if = {
					limit = { GRE = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
					GRE = {
						IKR = { get_current_government_type = yes }
						set_autonomy = {
							target = IKR
							autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_unilateral_union
						}
						IKR = {
							restore_previous_government_type = yes
							remove_ideas = standing_alone
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_core_of = SMS
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = SMS }
			}
			SMS = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_core_of = GRE
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SMS
						is_core_of = IKR
						is_core_of = ALB
					}
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = GRE }
			}
			GRE = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_core_of = GRE
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SMS
						is_core_of = IKR
						is_core_of = ALB
					}
				}
				country_exists = GRE
				GRE = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = GRE
				copy_tag = GRE
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}

				var:global.occupied_state = {

					is_core_of = GRE
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = SMS
						is_core_of = IKR

					}
				}

						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_assyrian_minority }
					is_core_of = ASY
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = ASY
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = ASY
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority }
					is_core_of = KUR
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = KUR }
			}
			KUR = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority }
					is_core_of = KUR
				}
				country_exists = KUR
				KUR = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = KUR
				copy_tag = KUR
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_kurdish_minority }
					is_core_of = KUR
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = KUR
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = KUR
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
					is_core_of = GEO
				}
				NOT = { country_exists = GEO }
			}
			GEO = {
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
					is_core_of = GEO
				}
				country_exists = GEO
				GEO = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
			}
			create_dynamic_country = {
				original_tag = GEO
				copy_tag = GEO
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_neutrality = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_democratic = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_fascism = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { allowed_party_communism = 1 }
				# do not change ideology of occupier country
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					remove_from_allowed_party = yes
				}
				if = {
					# if occupied country exists and different than new country
					# it is white peaced & subject of occupier. ignore its ideology as well
					limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = global.occupied_country } } }
					var:global.occupied_country = {
						remove_from_allowed_party = yes
					}
				}
				# change government if necesarry
				random_list = {
					allowed_party_democratic = {
						set_popularities = {
							democratic = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = democratic elections_allowed = yes }
					}
					allowed_party_fascism = {
						set_popularities = {
							fascism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_communism = {
						set_popularities = {
							communism = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = communism elections_allowed = no }
					}
					allowed_party_neutrality = {
						set_popularities = {
							neutrality = 100
						}
						set_politics = { ruling_party = neutrality elections_allowed = no }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.occupied_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
					is_core_of = GEO
				}
				any_country_with_original_tag = {
					original_tag_to_check = GEO
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
			}
			random_country_with_original_tag = {
				original_tag_to_check = GEO
				limit = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		every_possible_country = {
			random_select_amount = 1
			limit = { var:global.occupied_state = { is_core_of = PREV } }
			set_temp_variable = { global.occupied_country = THIS }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { country_exists = var:global.occupied_country } }
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = var:global.occupied_country
					var:global.occupied_country = { has_war_with = var:global.occupier_country }
				}
				transfer_state = var:global.occupied_state
				set_temp_variable = { global.new_occupied_country = THIS }
			}
		}
		var:global.new_occupied_country = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = standing_alone
				days = 270
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = created_civil_war_template } }
				set_country_flag = created_civil_war_template
				division_template = {
					name = "Resistance"
					is_locked = yes
					regiments = {
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						irregular_infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					}
				}
			}
			clear_temp_array = checked_neighbours
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					state = var:global.occupied_state
					impassable = no
				}
				# move our armies to back home
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ally_with = global.occupier_country
							has_military_access_to = global.occupier_country
						}
					}
					to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
				}
				# create resistance units, number is relative to size of industry
				set_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 100000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 200000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 300000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 400000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state_population > 500000 }
					add_to_temp_variable = { num_units_to_create = 1 } 
				}
				if = {
					limit = { var:global.occupier_country = { has_completed_focus = TUR_iron_fist_of_the_empire } }
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = num_units_to_create
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Resistance\" start_experience_factor = 0.4 start_equipment_factor = 0.4"
							owner = var:global.new_occupied_country
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					for_loop_effect = {
						end = num_units_to_create
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Resistance\" start_experience_factor = 0.6 start_equipment_factor = 0.6"
							owner = var:global.new_occupied_country
						}
					}
				}
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = num_units_to_create min = 1 max = 6 }
				# move our armies so they are not surrounded/create pockets
				every_neighbor_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = global.occupied_country
						is_core_of = global.occupied_country
						not = { is_in_array = { checked_neighbours = this } }
					}
					add_to_temp_array = { checked_neighbours = this }
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								is_ally_with = global.occupier_country
								has_military_access_to = global.occupier_country
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
					set_state_province_controller = {
						controller = global.occupied_country
						limit = { is_ally_with = global.occupier_country }
					}
				}
			}
			# create war if necesarry
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_war_with = global.occupier_country } }
				declare_war_on = { target = global.occupier_country type = annex_everything }
				set_country_flag = TUR_rebelling_country
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = MAC
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = { country_event = { id = ottoman.7 days = 3 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ALB
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					country_event = { id = ottoman.185 }
					country_event = { id = ottoman.7 days = 3 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = YEM
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = {
					country_event = { id = ottoman.186 }
					country_event = { id = ottoman.110 hours = 16 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ASR
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = { country_event = { id = ottoman.187 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = HJZ
					has_war_with = global.occupier_country
				}
				var:global.occupier_country = { country_event = { id = ottoman.188 } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				var:global.new_occupied_country = { original_tag = HJZ }
				var:global.occupier_country = { has_country_flag = TUR_arab_revolt }
			}
			set_global_flag = great_arabian_revolt
			news_event = { id = ww1_hejaz.8 hours = 6 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Elections of 1912
	id = ottoman.5
	title = ottoman.5.t
	desc = ottoman.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1912.6.1
		date < 1913.1.1
		has_elections = yes
		NOT = { has_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912 }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = TUR_neutrality_party_long
				name = TUR_neutrality_party
			}
		}
		TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes
		set_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity = TUR_neutrality_popularity }
		set_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity = TUR_democratic_popularity }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.5.a
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
			check_variable = { TUR_itf_popularity > TUR_hif_popularity }
		}
		TUR_mahmud_sevket = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		set_politics = {
		    ruling_party = neutrality
    	    election_frequency = 48
		    elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		set_country_flag = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory_elections
		complete_national_focus = TUR_elections_of_1912
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_cabinet_crisis }
			remove_ideas = TUR_cabinet_crisis
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_opposition_in_cabinet }
			remove_ideas = TUR_opposition_in_cabinet
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_revamped_cabined }
			remove_ideas = TUR_revamped_cabined
		}
		TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.5.b
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
			check_variable = { TUR_hif_popularity > TUR_itf_popularity }
		}
		promote_character = TUR_mehmed_kamil
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = democratic
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		set_country_flag = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory_elections
		complete_national_focus = TUR_elections_of_1912
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_cabinet_crisis }
			remove_ideas = TUR_cabinet_crisis
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_opposition_in_cabinet }
			remove_ideas = TUR_opposition_in_cabinet
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TUR_revamped_cabined }
			remove_ideas = TUR_revamped_cabined
		}
		TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.5.c
		trigger = { has_war = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = democratic }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = neutrality }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = fascism }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = communism }
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communism
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			tooltip = TUR_government_stability_reduce_5
			TUR_government_stability_var = -5
		}
		TUR_government_stability_calculate = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.5.tt
		set_country_flag = TUR_postpone_elections_cuz_of_war
		TUR_government_popularity_calculate = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
	}
}

country_event = { #saviour officer Coup
	id = ottoman.6
	title = ottoman.6.t
	desc = ottoman.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_saviour_officers_coup
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.6.a
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			name = TUR_saviour_officer
			long_name = TUR_saviour_officer
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = TUR_ahmed_muhtar
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				traits = { TUR_the_victorious grand_vizier }
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
				last_election = "1908.12.17"
				election_frequency = 48
				elections_allowed = yes
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_elections_to_be_held_later_tt

country_event = { #ottomans ask french to join them russia ask ottomans dominion
	id = ottoman.26
	title = ottoman.26.t
	desc = ottoman.26.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.26.a
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			add_to_faction = TUR
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_diplomatic_isolation_1
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_democratic_party_value
				value = party_popularity@democratic
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
				value = party_popularity@neutrality
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_communism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@communism
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = ottoman_fascism_party_value
				value = party_popularity@fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = democratic }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communism }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = neutrality }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = fascism }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_elections = yes }
				set_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = TUR
				autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				end_wars = yes
				end_civil_wars = no
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = democratic
				popularity = ottoman_democratic_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = ottoman_neutrality_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communism
				popularity = ottoman_communism_party_value
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = ottoman_fascism_party_value
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ottomans_are_democratic }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ottomans_are_communist }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					election_frequency = 48
					elections_allowed = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ottomans_are_neutrality
					NOT = { has_country_flag = ottomans_have_elections }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = ottomans_are_fascism }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.27 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.26.b
		hidden_effect = {
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						tag = RUS
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.28 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #permission of ottomans to invest
	id = ottoman.45
	title = ottoman.45.t
	desc = ottoman.45.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_ottoman_investments
	option = {
		name = ottoman.45.a
		TUR_investment_add_effect = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 15 } 
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.45.b
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = FRA } }
			remove_mission = TUR_investments_from_FRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = ENG } }
			remove_mission = TUR_investments_from_ENG
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = GER } }
			remove_mission = TUR_investments_from_GER
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = BEL } }
			remove_mission = TUR_investments_from_BEL
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { tag = HOL } }
			remove_mission = TUR_investments_from_HOL
		}

	}

						industrial_complex > 1
						arms_factory > 1
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_local_development }
					}
					TUR_state_has_minority = yes
				}
				set_variable = { ROOT.TUR_local_development_state_var = THIS }
			}
			country_event = ottoman.73
			clear_variable = ROOT.TUR_local_development_state_var
		}
		country_event = { id = ottoman.72 days = 180 random_days = 180 }
	}
}

country_event = { #frozen foreign assets add
	id = ottoman.108
	title = ottoman.108.t
	desc = ottoman.108.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_duyun_u_umumiye
	option = {
		name = ottoman.108.a
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				set_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_after_war = opda_consumer_goods }
				set_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite_after_war = opda_consumer_goods_opposite }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_remove_debt_current_amount_war
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = FROM.opda_consumer_goods_after_war }
			add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = FROM.opda_consumer_goods_opposite_after_war }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods
				min = 0
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
				max = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { FROM = { has_variable = opda_consumer_goods } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_current_amount_FROM_war
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods = opda_consumer_goods_opposite_after_war }
					add_to_variable = { opda_consumer_goods_opposite = opda_consumer_goods_after_war }
					clamp_variable = {
						var = opda_consumer_goods
						max = 0
					}
					clamp_variable = {
						var = opda_consumer_goods_opposite
						min = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		TUR_debt_value_check = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = ottoman.108.tt
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

	hidden = yes
	trigger = { has_completed_focus = TUR_autonomy_in_administration }
	immediate = {
		random_list = {
			25 = { #izmir
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 339
							controls_state = 824
							controls_state = 340
							controls_state = 342
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_izmir_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.115 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
			25 = { #trabzon
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 354
							controls_state = 355
							controls_state = 1034
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_trabzon_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.116 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
			25 = { #diyarbakir
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 350
							controls_state = 1028
							controls_state = 884
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_diyarbakir_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.117 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
			25 = { #edirne
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					OR = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 756
							controls_state = 341
							controls_state = 860
							controls_state = 200
							controls_state = 849
							controls_state = 757
							controls_state = 451
							controls_state = 212
						}
						has_country_flag = TUR_edirne_unionist_autonomy
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = ottoman.121 days = 70 random_days = 35 }
			}
		}
	}
}

					value = 0.1

			else = {

					value = 0.05
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
	}

	}

country_event = { #ottoman defeat in egypt
	id = ottoman.195
	title = ottoman.195.t
	desc = ottoman.195.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_ottomans_occupy_egypt
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = EGY
						has_war_together_with = EGY
					}
				}
				country_event = ottoman.196
			}
		}
	}
	trigger = {
		all_state = {
			is_core_of = EGY
			controller = { NOT = { has_war_with = EGY } }
		}
		surrender_progress > 0.05
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.195.a
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			white_peace = EGY
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						AND = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							has_autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_ottoman_committee_government
						}
					}
				}
				is_core_of = EGY
			}
			transfer_state_to = EGY
		}
		clr_global_flag = TUR_ottoman_invasion_of_egypt
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

			limit = { has_country_flag = yenikoy_accord_involved }
			country_event = { id = ottoman.215 hours = 8 }
		}
		event_option_tooltip = ottoman.215.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = GER }
					has_war_with = GER
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = FRA }
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = ENG }
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = { country_exists = ITA }
					has_war_with = ITA
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = RUS
					ratio > 3
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}
	}

country_event = { #yenikoy accord
	id = ottoman.215
	title = ottoman.215.t
	desc = ottoman.215.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_armenian_reforms
	option = { #russia
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			NOT = { has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise }
		}
		name = ottoman.215.a
		TUR_create_armenian_vilayet = yes
		set_global_flag = yenikoy_accord
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = { #russia
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise
		}
		name = ottoman.215.b
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				OR = {
					has_state_flag = TUR_trabzon
					has_state_flag = TUR_erzurum
					has_state_flag = TUR_sivas
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = TUR
				OR = {
					has_state_flag = TUR_van
					has_state_flag = TUR_bitlis
					has_state_flag = TUR_mamuret_ul_aziz
					has_state_flag = TUR_diyarbakir
				}
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_trabzon
						has_state_flag = TUR_erzurum
						has_state_flag = TUR_sivas
						has_state_flag = TUR_van
						has_state_flag = TUR_bitlis
						has_state_flag = TUR_mamuret_ul_aziz
						has_state_flag = TUR_diyarbakir
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = TUR_yenikoy_accord
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = TUR } }
					set_state_flag = TUR_autonomous_vilayet_no_control
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = yenikoy_accord
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = { #ottomans
		trigger = { original_tag = TUR }
		name = ottoman.215.c
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise }
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_trabzon
							has_state_flag = TUR_erzurum
							has_state_flag = TUR_sivas
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_van
							has_state_flag = TUR_bitlis
							has_state_flag = TUR_mamuret_ul_aziz
							has_state_flag = TUR_diyarbakir
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { effect_tooltip = { TUR_create_armenian_vilayet = yes = yes } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = { #foreign power
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = TUR
				original_tag = RUS
			}
		}
		name = ottoman.215.e
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = yenikoy_accord_compromise }
			effect_tooltip = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_trabzon
							has_state_flag = TUR_erzurum
							has_state_flag = TUR_sivas
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
						OR = {
							has_state_flag = TUR_van
							has_state_flag = TUR_bitlis
							has_state_flag = TUR_mamuret_ul_aziz
							has_state_flag = TUR_diyarbakir
						}
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_vilayet }
				}
			}
		}
		else = { effect_tooltip = { TUR_create_armenian_vilayet = yes = yes } }
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}
